  262. 138. Mathbox for Kunhao Zheng
    1. 138.1. Weighted AM-GM inequality

MetaMath theorems

Lebesgue measure on n-dimensional Real numbers

Constants


voln*

Extend class notation with the class of Lebesgue outer measure for the space of multidimensional real numbers.

Axiom: covoln


class voln*

Disjoint


x y z i j k

Define the outer measure for the space of multidimensional real numbers. The cardinality of x is the dimension of the space modeled. Definition 115C of [Fremlin1] p. 30. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 11-Oct-2020.)

Axiom: df-ovoln


|- voln* = ( x e. Fin |-> ( y e. ~P ( RR ^m x ) |-> if ( x = (/) , 0 , inf ( { z e. RR* | E. i e. ( ( ( RR X. RR ) ^m x ) ^m NN ) ( y C_ U_ j e. NN X_ k e. x ( ( [,) o. ( i ` j ) ) ` k ) /\ z = ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> prod_ k e. x ( vol ` ( ( [,) o. ( i ` j ) ) ` k ) ) ) ) ) } , RR* , < ) ) ) )

Constants


voln

Extend class notation with the class of Lebesgue measure for the space of multidimensional real numbers.

Axiom: cvoln


class voln

Define the Lebesgue measure for the space of multidimensional real numbers. The cardinality of x is the dimension of the space modeled. Definition 115C of [Fremlin1] p. 30. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 11-Oct-2020.)

Axiom: df-voln


|- voln = ( x e. Fin |-> ( ( voln* ` x ) |` ( CaraGen ` ( voln* ` x ) ) ) )

Disjoint


X x

Disjoint


ph x

Essential: vonval.1


|- ( ph -> X e. Fin )

Value of the Lebesgue measure for a given finite dimension. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 11-Oct-2020.)

Theorem: vonval


|- ( ph -> ( voln ` X ) = ( ( voln* ` X ) |` ( CaraGen ` ( voln* ` X ) ) ) )

Essential: ovnlecvr.ss

Given a subset of multidimensional reals and a set of half-open intervals that covers it, the Lebesgue outer measure of the set is bounded by the generalized sum of the pre-measure of the half-open intervals. The statement would also be true with X the empty set, but covers are not used for the zero-dimensional case. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 11-Oct-2020.)

Essential: hoidmv1lelem3.s


|- S = sup ( U , RR , < )

The dimensional volume of a 1-dimensional half-open interval is less than or equal the generalized sum of the dimensional volumes of countable half-open intervals that cover it. This is the non-empty, finite generalized sum, sub case in Lemma 114B of [Fremlin1] p. 23. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Essential: hoidmv1le.s


|- ( ph -> X_ k e. X ( ( A ` k ) [,) ( B ` k ) ) C_ U_ j e. NN X_ k e. X ( ( ( C ` j ) ` k ) [,) ( ( D ` j ) ` k ) ) )

The dimensional volume of a 1-dimensional half-open interval is less than or equal to the generalized sum of the dimensional volumes of countable half-open intervals that cover it. This is one of the two base cases of the induction of Lemma 115B of [Fremlin1] p. 29 (the other base case is the 0-dimensional case). This proof of the 1-dimensional case is given in Lemma 114B of [Fremlin1] p. 23. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.l


|- L = ( x e. Fin |-> ( a e. ( RR ^m x ) , b e. ( RR ^m x ) |-> if ( x = (/) , 0 , prod_ k e. x ( vol ` ( ( a ` k ) [,) ( b ` k ) ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.x


|- ( ph -> X e. Fin )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.y


|- ( ph -> Y C_ X )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.z


|- ( ph -> Z e. ( X \ Y ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.w


|- W = ( Y u. { Z } )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.a


|- ( ph -> A : W --> RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.b


|- ( ph -> B : W --> RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.c


|- ( ph -> C : NN --> ( RR ^m W ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.d


|- ( ph -> D : NN --> ( RR ^m W ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.r


|- ( ph -> ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( D ` j ) ) ) ) e. RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.h


|- H = ( x e. RR |-> ( c e. ( RR ^m W ) |-> ( j e. W |-> if ( j e. Y , ( c ` j ) , if ( ( c ` j ) <_ x , ( c ` j ) , x ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.g


|- G = ( ( A |` Y ) ( L ` Y ) ( B |` Y ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.e


|- ( ph -> E e. RR+ )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.u


|- U = { z e. ( ( A ` Z ) [,] ( B ` Z ) ) | ( G x. ( z - ( A ` Z ) ) ) <_ ( ( 1 + E ) x. ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( ( H ` z ) ` ( D ` j ) ) ) ) ) ) }

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.s


|- S = sup ( U , RR , < )

Essential: hoidmvlelem1.ab


|- ( ph -> ( A ` Z ) < ( B ` Z ) )

The supremum of U belongs to U . Step (c) in the proof of Lemma 115B of [Fremlin1] p. 29. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

|- ( ph -> S e. U )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.l


|- L = ( x e. Fin |-> ( a e. ( RR ^m x ) , b e. ( RR ^m x ) |-> if ( x = (/) , 0 , prod_ k e. x ( vol ` ( ( a ` k ) [,) ( b ` k ) ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.x


|- ( ph -> X e. Fin )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.y


|- ( ph -> Y C_ X )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.z


|- ( ph -> Z e. ( X \ Y ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.w


|- W = ( Y u. { Z } )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.a


|- ( ph -> A : W --> RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.b


|- ( ph -> B : W --> RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.c


|- ( ph -> C : NN --> ( RR ^m W ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.f


|- F = ( y e. Y |-> 0 )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.j


|- J = ( j e. NN |-> if ( S e. ( ( ( C ` j ) ` Z ) [,) ( ( D ` j ) ` Z ) ) , ( ( C ` j ) |` Y ) , F ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.d


|- ( ph -> D : NN --> ( RR ^m W ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.k


|- K = ( j e. NN |-> if ( S e. ( ( ( C ` j ) ` Z ) [,) ( ( D ` j ) ` Z ) ) , ( ( D ` j ) |` Y ) , F ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.r


|- ( ph -> ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( D ` j ) ) ) ) e. RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.h


|- H = ( x e. RR |-> ( c e. ( RR ^m W ) |-> ( j e. W |-> if ( j e. Y , ( c ` j ) , if ( ( c ` j ) <_ x , ( c ` j ) , x ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.g


|- G = ( ( A |` Y ) ( L ` Y ) ( B |` Y ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.e


|- ( ph -> E e. RR+ )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.u


|- U = { z e. ( ( A ` Z ) [,] ( B ` Z ) ) | ( G x. ( z - ( A ` Z ) ) ) <_ ( ( 1 + E ) x. ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( ( H ` z ) ` ( D ` j ) ) ) ) ) ) }

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.su


|- ( ph -> S e. U )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.sb


|- ( ph -> S < ( B ` Z ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.p


|- P = ( j e. NN |-> ( ( J ` j ) ( L ` Y ) ( K ` j ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.m


|- ( ph -> M e. NN )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.le


|- ( ph -> G <_ ( ( 1 + E ) x. sum_ j e. ( 1 ... M ) ( P ` j ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.O


|- O = ran ( i e. { j e. ( 1 ... M ) | S e. ( ( ( C ` j ) ` Z ) [,) ( ( D ` j ) ` Z ) ) } |-> ( ( D ` i ) ` Z ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.v


|- V = ( { ( B ` Z ) } u. O )

Essential: hoidmvlelem2.q


|- Q = inf ( V , RR , < )

This is the contradiction proven in step (d) in the proof of Lemma 115B of [Fremlin1] p. 29. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Essential: hoidmvlelem3.l


|- L = ( x e. Fin |-> ( a e. ( RR ^m x ) , b e. ( RR ^m x ) |-> if ( x = (/) , 0 , prod_ k e. x ( vol ` ( ( a ` k ) [,) ( b ` k ) ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem3.z

|- L = ( x e. Fin |-> ( a e. ( RR ^m x ) , b e. ( RR ^m x ) |-> if ( x = (/) , 0 , prod_ k e. x ( vol ` ( ( a ` k ) [,) ( b ` k ) ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.n

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.z

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.w

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.a

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.b

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.k

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.d

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.r


|- ( ph -> ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( D ` j ) ) ) ) e. RR )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.h


|- H = ( x e. RR |-> ( c e. ( RR ^m W ) |-> ( j e. W |-> if ( j e. Y , ( c ` j ) , if ( ( c ` j ) <_ x , ( c ` j ) , x ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.14


|- G = ( ( A |` Y ) ( L ` Y ) ( B |` Y ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.e


|- ( ph -> E e. RR+ )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.u


|- U = { z e. ( ( A ` Z ) [,] ( B ` Z ) ) | ( G x. ( z - ( A ` Z ) ) ) <_ ( ( 1 + E ) x. ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( ( H ` z ) ` ( D ` j ) ) ) ) ) ) }

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.s


|- S = sup ( U , RR , < )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.i


|- ( ph -> A. e e. ( RR ^m Y ) A. f e. ( RR ^m Y ) A. g e. ( ( RR ^m Y ) ^m NN ) A. h e. ( ( RR ^m Y ) ^m NN ) ( X_ k e. Y ( ( e ` k ) [,) ( f ` k ) ) C_ U_ j e. NN X_ k e. Y ( ( ( g ` j ) ` k ) [,) ( ( h ` j ) ` k ) ) -> ( e ( L ` Y ) f ) <_ ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( g ` j ) ( L ` Y ) ( h ` j ) ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hoidmvlelem4.i2


|- ( ph -> X_ k e. W ( ( A ` k ) [,) ( B ` k ) ) C_ U_ j e. NN X_ k e. W ( ( ( C ` j ) ` k ) [,) ( ( D ` j ) ` k ) ) )

The dimensional volume of a multidimensional half-open interval is less than or equal the generalized sum of the dimensional volumes of countable half-open intervals that cover it. Induction step of Lemma 115B of [Fremlin1] p. 29, case nonempty interval and dimension of the space greater than 1 . (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Theorem: hoidmvlelem4


|- ( ph -> ( A ( L ` W ) B ) <_ ( ( 1 + E ) x. ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> ( ( C ` j ) ( L ` W ) ( D ` j ) ) ) ) ) )

The dimensional volume of a multidimensional half-open interval is less than or equal the generalized sum of the dimensional volumes of countable half-open intervals that cover it. Induction step of Lemma 115B of [Fremlin1] p. 29. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Essential: ovnhoilem1.c


|- I = X_ k e. X ( ( A ` k ) [,) ( B ` k ) )

Essential: ovnhoilem1.m


|- M = { z e. RR* | E. i e. ( ( ( RR X. RR ) ^m X ) ^m NN ) ( I C_ U_ j e. NN X_ k e. X ( ( [,) o. ( i ` j ) ) ` k ) /\ z = ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> prod_ k e. X ( vol ` ( ( [,) o. ( i ` j ) ) ` k ) ) ) ) ) }

Essential: ovnhoilem1.h


|- H = ( j e. NN |-> ( k e. X |-> if ( j = 1 , <. ( A ` k ) , ( B ` k ) >. , <. 0 , 0 >. ) ) )

The Lebesgue outer measure of a multidimensional half-open interval is less than or equal to the product of its length in each dimension. First part of the proof of Proposition 115D (b) of [Fremlin1] p. 30. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Theorem: ovnhoilem1


|- ( ph -> ( ( voln* ` X ) ` I ) <_ prod_ k e. X ( vol ` ( ( A ` k ) [,) ( B ` k ) ) ) )

The Lebesgue outer measure of a multidimensional half-open interval is less than or equal to the product of its length in each dimension. Second part of the proof of Proposition 115D (b) of [Fremlin1] p. 30. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 21-Nov-2020.)

Essential: hspmbllem2.h


|- H = ( x e. Fin |-> ( l e. x , y e. RR |-> X_ k e. x if ( k = l , ( -oo (,) y ) , RR ) ) )

Essential: hspmbllem2.x


|- ( ph -> X e. Fin )

Essential: hspmbllem2.k


|- ( ph -> K e. X )

Essential: hspmbllem2.y

Essential: hspmbllem2.e

Essential: hspmbllem2.c

Essential: hspmbllem2.d

Essential: hspmbllem2.a

Essential: hspmbllem2.g


|- ( ph -> ( sum^ ` ( j e. NN |-> prod_ k e. X ( vol ` ( ( ( C ` j ) ` k ) [,) ( ( D ` j ) ` k ) ) ) ) ) <_ ( ( ( voln* ` X ) ` A ) + E ) )

Essential: hspmbllem2.r

Essential: hspmbllem2.i

Essential: hspmbllem2.f


|- ( ph -> ( ( voln* ` X ) ` ( A \ ( K ( H ` X ) Y ) ) ) e. RR )

Essential: hspmbllem2.l


|- L = ( x e. Fin |-> ( a e. ( RR ^m x ) , b e. ( RR ^m x ) |-> if ( x = (/) , 0 , prod_ k e. x ( vol ` ( ( a ` k ) [,) ( b ` k ) ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hspmbllem2.t


|- T = ( y e. RR |-> ( c e. ( RR ^m X ) |-> ( h e. X |-> if ( h e. ( X \ { K } ) , ( c ` h ) , if ( ( c ` h ) <_ y , ( c ` h ) , y ) ) ) ) )

Essential: hspmbllem2.s


|- S = ( x e. RR |-> ( c e. ( RR ^m X ) |-> ( h e. X |-> if ( h = K , if ( x <_ ( c ` h ) , ( c ` h ) , x ) , ( c ` h ) ) ) ) )

Any half-space of the n-dimensional Real numbers is Lebesgue measurable. This is Step (b) of Lemma 115F of [Fremlin1] p. 31. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 24-Dec-2020.)

Theorem: hspmbllem2


|- ( ph -> ( ( ( voln* ` X ) ` ( A i^i ( K ( H ` X ) Y ) ) ) + ( ( voln* ` X ) ` ( A \ ( K ( H ` X ) Y ) ) ) ) <_ ( ( ( voln* ` X ) ` A ) + E ) )

Essential: isvonmbl.1


|- ( ph -> X e. Fin )

The predicate " A is measurable w.r.t. the n-dimensional Lebesgue measure". A set is measurable if it splits every other set x in a "nice" way, that is, if the measure of the pieces x i^i A and x \ A sum up to the measure of x . Definition 114E of [Fremlin1] p. 25. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 3-Mar-2021.)

The sequence of the measures of the half-open intervals converges to the measure of their intersection. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 8-Apr-2021.)
